+    sum_sq += v0 * v0
 
+    v1 = S.convert(y[row, c1], S.f32)
+    sum_val += v1
+    sum_sq += v1 * v1
+
+    partial[tid] = sum_val
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    stride = 128
+    for _ in S.range(8):
+        if tid < stride:
+            partial[tid] = partial[tid] + partial[tid + stride]
+        S.syncthreads()
+        stride = stride >> 0x1
+
+    mean = partial[0] / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+    partial[tid] = sum_sq
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    stride = 128
+    for _ in S.range(8):
+        if tid < stride:
+            partial[tid] = partial[tid] + partial[tid + stride]
+        S.syncthreads()
+        stride = stride >> 0x1
+
+    mean_sq = partial[0] / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+    var = mean_sq - mean * mean
+    denom = S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
+
+    n0 = (v0 - mean) / denom
+    n0 = n0 * S.convert(gn_weight[c0], S.f32) + S.convert(gn_bias[c0], S.f32)
+    if n0 < S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32):
+        n0 = S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32)
+    if n0 > S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32):
+        n0 = S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32)
+    y[row, c0] = S.convert(n0, S.bf16)
+
+    n1 = (v1 - mean) / denom
+    n1 = n1 * S.convert(gn_weight[c1], S.f32) + S.convert(gn_bias[c1], S.f32)
+    if n1 < S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32):
+        n1 = S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32)
+    if n1 > S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32):
+        n1 = S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32)
+    y[row, c1] = S.convert(n1, S.bf16)

+def _pack_a(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    xb = x.view(BATCH_SIZE // WARP_M, WARP_M, IN_FEATURES // K_TILE, K_TILE).permute(0, 2, 1, 3)
+    first = torch.cat((xb[:, :, :, 0:4], xb[:, :, :, 8:12]), dim=-1)
+    second = torch.cat((xb[:, :, :, 4:8], xb[:, :, :, 12:16]), dim=-1)
+    return torch.cat((first, second), dim=2).contiguous()
+
+
+def _pack_b(w: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    wb = w.view(IN_FEATURES // K_TILE, K_TILE, OUT_FEATURES // WARP_N, WARP_N).permute(0, 2, 1, 3)
+    groups = []
+    for g in range(WARP_N // 4):
+        cols = wb[:, :, :, g * 4 : (g + 1) * 4]
+        groups.append(torch.cat((cols[:, :, 0:8, :], cols[:, :, 8:16, :]), dim=1))
+    return torch.cat(groups, dim=2).contiguous()

 HARDTANH_MAX = 2.0
 EPS = 1e-05
 
+WARP_SIZE = 64
+NUM_WARPS = 4
+BLOCK_THREADS = WARP_SIZE * NUM_WARPS
+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+WARP_M = 32
+WARP_N = 32
+K_TILE = 16
+
+A_PACK_M = BATCH_SIZE // WARP_M
+A_PACK_K = IN_FEATURES // K_TILE
+B_PACK_K = IN_FEATURES // K_TILE
+B_PACK_N = OUT_FEATURES // WARP_N
+
+A_PACK_RANGE_BYTES = A_PACK_M * A_PACK_K * WARP_SIZE * 8 * 2
+B_PACK_RANGE_BYTES = B_PACK_K * B_PACK_N * WARP_SIZE * 8 * 2
+
+
+def _launch_gemm():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (BLOCK_THREADS, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _launch_post():
+    return ((NUM_GROUPS, BATCH_SIZE, 1), (256, 1, 1))

+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_mfma_kernel(
+    a_pack: S.Tensor((A_PACK_M, A_PACK_K, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16),
+    b_pack: S.Tensor((B_PACK_K, B_PACK_N, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16),
+    bias: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WARP_SIZE
+    warp = tid // WARP_SIZE
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2
+
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    tile_row = block_row + warp_row * WARP_M
+    tile_col = block_col + warp_col * WARP_N
+
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(a_pack, A_PACK_RANGE_BYTES)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(b_pack, B_PACK_RANGE_BYTES)
+
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    a_smem = S.make_shared((NUM_WARPS, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((NUM_WARPS, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16)
+
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(A_PACK_K):
+        a_elem_offset = (((tile_row // WARP_M) * A_PACK_K + k_tile) * WARP_SIZE + lane) * 8
+        b_elem_offset = ((k_tile * B_PACK_N + (tile_col // WARP_N)) * WARP_SIZE + lane) * 8
+        a_byte_offset = S.convert(a_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+        b_byte_offset = S.convert(b_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+
+        a_frag_g = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, a_byte_offset, 0)
+        b_frag_g = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_byte_offset, 0)
+
+        a_frag_view = S.view(a_frag_g, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag_view = S.view(b_frag_g, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        for frag_half in S.range(2):
+            for frag_elem in S.range(4):
+                a_smem[warp, lane, frag_half * 4 + frag_elem] = a_frag_view[frag_half, frag_elem, 0]
+                b_smem[warp, lane, frag_half * 4 + frag_elem] = b_frag_view[frag_half, frag_elem, 0]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        m_a = S.full((2, 4, 1), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        m_b = S.full((2, 4, 1), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        for frag_half in S.range(2):
+            for frag_elem in S.range(4):
+                m_a[frag_half, frag_elem, 0] = a_smem[warp, lane, frag_half * 4 + frag_elem]
+                m_b[frag_half, frag_elem, 0] = b_smem[warp, lane, frag_half * 4 + frag_elem]
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    lane_col = lane % 32
+    lane_row_quad = lane // 32
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        out_col = tile_col + lane_col
+        out_row = tile_row + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * lane_row_quad + (acc_idx % 4)
+        value = acc[acc_idx] + S.convert(bias[out_col], S.f32)
+        y[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(value, S.bf16)

codex
The remaining blocker is the slice expression passed into MFMA. I’m replacing the `m_a[0]`/`m_a[1]` style views with explicit 4-element BF16 fragments, which should match the intrinsic signature more directly.

+def gemm_mfma_kernel(
+    a_pack: S.Tensor((A_PACK_M, A_PACK_K, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16),
+    b_pack: S.Tensor((B_PACK_K, B_PACK_N, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16),
+    bias: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WARP_SIZE
+    warp = tid // WARP_SIZE
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2
+
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    tile_row = block_row + warp_row * WARP_M
+    tile_col = block_col + warp_col * WARP_N
+
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(a_pack, A_PACK_RANGE_BYTES)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(b_pack, B_PACK_RANGE_BYTES)
+
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    a_smem = S.make_shared((NUM_WARPS, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((NUM_WARPS, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16)
+
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(A_PACK_K):
+        a_elem_offset = (((tile_row // WARP_M) * A_PACK_K + k_tile) * WARP_SIZE + lane) * 8
+        b_elem_offset = ((k_tile * B_PACK_N + (tile_col // WARP_N)) * WARP_SIZE + lane) * 8
+        a_byte_offset = S.convert(a_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+        b_byte_offset = S.convert(b_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+
+        a_frag_g = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, a_byte_offset, 0)
+        b_frag_g = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_byte_offset, 0)
+
+        a_frag_view = S.view(a_frag_g, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag_view = S.view(b_frag_g, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        for frag_half in S.range(2):
+            for frag_elem in S.range(4):
+                a_smem[warp, lane, frag_half * 4 + frag_elem] = a_frag_view[frag_half, frag_elem, 0]
+                b_smem[warp, lane, frag_half * 4 + frag_elem] = b_frag_view[frag_half, frag_elem, 0]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a0 = S.full((4, 1), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        a1 = S.full((4, 1), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        b0 = S.full((4, 1), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        b1 = S.full((4, 1), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        for frag_elem in S.range(4):
+            a0[frag_elem, 0] = a_smem[warp, lane, frag_elem]
+            a1[frag_elem, 0] = a_smem[warp, lane, 4 + frag_elem]
+            b0[frag_elem, 0] = b_smem[warp, lane, frag_elem]
+            b1[frag_elem, 0] = b_smem[warp, lane, 4 + frag_elem]
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a0, b0, acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a1, b1, acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    lane_col = lane % 32
+    lane_row_quad = lane // 32
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        out_col = tile_col + lane_col
+        out_row = tile_row + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * lane_row_quad + (acc_idx % 4)
+        value = acc[acc_idx] + S.convert(bias[out_col], S.f32)
+        y[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(value, S.bf16)
+

+@substrate.jit
+def groupnorm_hardtanh_kernel(
+    y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    gn_weight: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    gn_bias: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    row = S.block_id(1)
+    group = S.block_id(0)
+    c0 = group * GROUP_SIZE + tid
+    c1 = c0 + 256
+
+    partial = S.make_shared((256,), S.f32)
+
+    sum_val = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+    sum_sq = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+
+    v0 = S.convert(y[row, c0], S.f32)
+    sum_val += v0
+    sum_sq += v0 * v0
+
+    v1 = S.convert(y[row, c1], S.f32)
+    sum_val += v1
+    sum_sq += v1 * v1
+
+    partial[tid] = sum_val
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    stride = 128
+    for _ in S.range(8):
+        if tid < stride:
+            partial[tid] = partial[tid] + partial[tid + stride]
+        S.syncthreads()
+        stride = stride >> 0x1
+
+    mean = partial[0] / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+    partial[tid] = sum_sq
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    stride = 128
+    for _ in S.range(8):
+        if tid < stride:
+            partial[tid] = partial[tid] + partial[tid + stride]
+        S.syncthreads()
+        stride = stride >> 0x1
+
+    mean_sq = partial[0] / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+    var = mean_sq - mean * mean
+    denom = S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))

+    if n0 > S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32):
+        n0 = S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32)
+    y[row, c0] = S.convert(n0, S.bf16)
 
+    n1 = (v1 - mean) / denom
+    n1 = n1 * S.convert(gn_weight[c1], S.f32) + S.convert(gn_bias[c1], S.f32)

+    y[row, c1] = S.convert(n1, S.bf16)

+def _pack_a(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    xb = x.view(BATCH_SIZE // WARP_M, WARP_M, IN_FEATURES // K_TILE, K_TILE).permute(0, 2, 1, 3)
+    first = torch.cat((xb[:, :, :, 0:4], xb[:, :, :, 8:12]), dim=-1)
+    second = torch.cat((xb[:, :, :, 4:8], xb[:, :, :, 12:16]), dim=-1)
+    return torch.cat((first, second), dim=2).contiguous()
+
+
+def _pack_b(w: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    wb = w.view(IN_FEATURES // K_TILE, K_TILE, OUT_FEATURES // WARP_N, WARP_N).permute(0, 2, 1, 3)
+    groups = []
+    for g in range(WARP_N // 4):
+        cols = wb[:, :, :, g * 4 : (g + 1) * 4]
+        groups.append(torch.cat((cols[:, :, 0:8, :], cols[:, :, 8:16, :]), dim=1))
+    return torch.cat(groups, dim=2).contiguous()
+

     def __init__(self, in_features, out_features, num_groups, hardtanh_min, hardtanh_max):

+def gemm_mfma_kernel(
+    a_pack: S.Tensor((A_PACK_M, A_PACK_K, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16),
+    b_pack: S.Tensor((B_PACK_K, B_PACK_N, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16),
+    bias: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WARP_SIZE
+    warp = tid // WARP_SIZE
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2
+
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    tile_row = block_row + warp_row * WARP_M
+    tile_col = block_col + warp_col * WARP_N
+
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(a_pack, A_PACK_RANGE_BYTES)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(b_pack, B_PACK_RANGE_BYTES)
+
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    a_smem = S.make_shared((NUM_WARPS, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((NUM_WARPS, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16)
+
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(A_PACK_K):
+        a_elem_offset = (((tile_row // WARP_M) * A_PACK_K + k_tile) * WARP_SIZE + lane) * 8
+        b_elem_offset = ((k_tile * B_PACK_N + (tile_col // WARP_N)) * WARP_SIZE + lane) * 8
+        a_byte_offset = S.convert(a_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+        b_byte_offset = S.convert(b_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+
+        a_frag_g = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, a_byte_offset, 0)
+        b_frag_g = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_byte_offset, 0)
+
+        a_frag_view = S.view(a_frag_g, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag_view = S.view(b_frag_g, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        for frag_half in S.range(2):
+            for frag_elem in S.range(4):
+                a_smem[warp, lane, frag_half * 4 + frag_elem] = a_frag_view[frag_half, frag_elem, 0]
+                b_smem[warp, lane, frag_half * 4 + frag_elem] = b_frag_view[frag_half, frag_elem, 0]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a0 = S.full((4, 1), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        a1 = S.full((4, 1), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        b0 = S.full((4, 1), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        b1 = S.full((4, 1), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        for frag_elem in S.range(4):
+            a0[frag_elem, 0] = a_smem[warp, lane, frag_elem]
+            a1[frag_elem, 0] = a_smem[warp, lane, 4 + frag_elem]
+            b0[frag_elem, 0] = b_smem[warp, lane, frag_elem]
+            b1[frag_elem, 0] = b_smem[warp, lane, 4 + frag_elem]
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a0, b0, acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a1, b1, acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    lane_col = lane % 32
+    lane_row_quad = lane // 32
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        out_col = tile_col + lane_col
+        out_row = tile_row + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * lane_row_quad + (acc_idx % 4)
+        value = acc[acc_idx] + S.convert(bias[out_col], S.f32)
+        y[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(value, S.bf16)
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def groupnorm_hardtanh_kernel(
+    y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    gn_weight: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    gn_bias: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    row = S.block_id(1)
+    group = S.block_id(0)
+    c0 = group * GROUP_SIZE + tid
+    c1 = c0 + 256
+
+    partial = S.make_shared((256,), S.f32)
+
+    sum_val = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+    sum_sq = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+
+    v0 = S.convert(y[row, c0], S.f32)
+    sum_val += v0
+    sum_sq += v0 * v0
+
+    v1 = S.convert(y[row, c1], S.f32)
+    sum_val += v1
+    sum_sq += v1 * v1
+
+    partial[tid] = sum_val
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    stride = 128
+    for _ in S.range(8):
+        if tid < stride:
+            partial[tid] = partial[tid] + partial[tid + stride]
+        S.syncthreads()
+        stride = stride >> 0x1
+
+    mean = partial[0] / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+    partial[tid] = sum_sq
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    stride = 128
+    for _ in S.range(8):
+        if tid < stride:
+            partial[tid] = partial[tid] + partial[tid + stride]
+        S.syncthreads()
+        stride = stride >> 0x1
+
+    mean_sq = partial[0] / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+    var = mean_sq - mean * mean
+    denom = S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
 
-class ModelNew(nn.Module):
+    n0 = (v0 - mean) / denom
+    n0 = n0 * S.convert(gn_weight[c0], S.f32) + S.convert(gn_bias[c0], S.f32)
+    if n0 < S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32):
+        n0 = S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32)
+    if n0 > S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32):
+        n0 = S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32)
+    y[row, c0] = S.convert(n0, S.bf16)
 
+    n1 = (v1 - mean) / denom
+    n1 = n1 * S.convert(gn_weight[c1], S.f32) + S.convert(gn_bias[c1], S.f32)
+    if n1 < S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32):
+        n1 = S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32)
+    if n1 > S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32):
+        n1 = S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32)
+    y[row, c1] = S.convert(n1, S.bf16)

+def _pack_a(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    xb = x.view(BATCH_SIZE // WARP_M, WARP_M, IN_FEATURES // K_TILE, K_TILE).permute(0, 2, 1, 3)
+    first = torch.cat((xb[:, :, :, 0:4], xb[:, :, :, 8:12]), dim=-1)
+    second = torch.cat((xb[:, :, :, 4:8], xb[:, :, :, 12:16]), dim=-1)
+    return torch.cat((first, second), dim=2).contiguous()
+
+
+def _pack_b(w: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    wb = w.view(IN_FEATURES // K_TILE, K_TILE, OUT_FEATURES // WARP_N, WARP_N).permute(0, 2, 1, 3)
+    groups = []
+    for g in range(WARP_N // 4):
+        cols = wb[:, :, :, g * 4 : (g + 1) * 4]
+        groups.append(torch.cat((cols[:, :, 0:8, :], cols[:, :, 8:16, :]), dim=1))
+    return torch.cat(groups, dim=2).contiguous()
+

+class ModelNew(nn.Module):
     def __init__(self, in_features, out_features, num_groups, hardtanh_min, hardtanh_max):
         super().__init__()
         self.gemm = nn.Linear(in_features, out_features)
         self.group_norm = nn.GroupNorm(num_groups, out_features)
         self.hardtanh = nn.Hardtanh(min_val=hardtanh_min, max_val=hardtanh_max)
+        self._cached_weight_ptr = None
+        self._cached_bias_ptr = None
+        self._cached_gn_weight_ptr = None
+        self._cached_gn_bias_ptr = None
+        self._b_pack = None
+        self._bias = None
+        self._gn_weight = None
+        self._gn_bias = None
+        self._y = None
 
+    def _refresh_static_buffers(self, device, dtype):
+        w = self.gemm.weight
+        b = self.gemm.bias
+        gw = self.group_norm.weight
+        gb = self.group_norm.bias
+
+        w_ptr = w.untyped_storage().data_ptr()
+        b_ptr = b.untyped_storage().data_ptr()
+        gw_ptr = gw.untyped_storage().data_ptr()
+        gb_ptr = gb.untyped_storage().data_ptr()
+
+        if (
+            self._b_pack is None
+            or self._cached_weight_ptr != w_ptr
+            or self._b_pack.device != device
+            or self._b_pack.dtype != dtype
+        ):
+            w_t = w.t().to(device=device, dtype=dtype).contiguous()
+            self._b_pack = _pack_b(w_t)
+            self._cached_weight_ptr = w_ptr
+
+        if (
+            self._bias is None
+            or self._cached_bias_ptr != b_ptr
+            or self._bias.device != device
+            or self._bias.dtype != dtype
+        ):
+            self._bias = b.to(device=device, dtype=dtype).contiguous()
+            self._cached_bias_ptr = b_ptr
+
+        if (
+            self._gn_weight is None
+            or self._cached_gn_weight_ptr != gw_ptr
+            or self._gn_weight.device != device
+            or self._gn_weight.dtype != dtype
+        ):
+            self._gn_weight = gw.to(device=device, dtype=dtype).contiguous()
+            self._cached_gn_weight_ptr = gw_ptr
+
+        if (
+            self._gn_bias is None
+            or self._cached_gn_bias_ptr != gb_ptr
+            or self._gn_bias.device != device
+            or self._gn_bias.dtype != dtype
+        ):
+            self._gn_bias = gb.to(device=device, dtype=dtype).contiguous()
+            self._cached_gn_bias_ptr = gb_ptr
+
+        if self._y is None or self._y.device != device or self._y.dtype != dtype:
+            self._y = torch.empty((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), device=device, dtype=dtype)
+

+        n0 = S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32)
+    if n0 > S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32):
+        n0 = S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32)
+    y[row, c0] = S.convert(n0, S.bf16)

+    y[row, c1] = S.convert(n1, S.bf16)

+def _pack_a(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    xb = x.view(BATCH_SIZE // WARP_M, WARP_M, IN_FEATURES // K_TILE, K_TILE).permute(0, 2, 1, 3)
+    first = torch.cat((xb[:, :, :, 0:4], xb[:, :, :, 8:12]), dim=-1)
+    second = torch.cat((xb[:, :, :, 4:8], xb[:, :, :, 12:16]), dim=-1)
+    return torch.cat((first, second), dim=2).contiguous()
+
+
+def _pack_b(w: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    wb = w.view(IN_FEATURES // K_TILE, K_TILE, OUT_FEATURES // WARP_N, WARP_N).permute(0, 2, 1, 3)
+    groups = []
+    for g in range(WARP_N // 4):
+        cols = wb[:, :, :, g * 4 : (g + 1) * 4]
+        groups.append(torch.cat((cols[:, :, 0:8, :], cols[:, :, 8:16, :]), dim=1))
+    return torch.cat(groups, dim=2).contiguous()

+WARP_SIZE = 64
+NUM_WARPS = 4
+BLOCK_THREADS = WARP_SIZE * NUM_WARPS
+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+WARP_M = 32
+WARP_N = 32
+K_TILE = 16
+
+A_PACK_M = BATCH_SIZE // WARP_M
+A_PACK_K = IN_FEATURES // K_TILE
+B_PACK_K = IN_FEATURES // K_TILE
+B_PACK_N = OUT_FEATURES // WARP_N
+
+A_PACK_RANGE_BYTES = A_PACK_M * A_PACK_K * WARP_SIZE * 8 * 2
+B_PACK_RANGE_BYTES = B_PACK_K * B_PACK_N * WARP_SIZE * 8 * 2

+def _launch_gemm():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (BLOCK_THREADS, 1, 1))

+def gemm_mfma_kernel(
+    a_pack: S.Tensor((A_PACK_M, A_PACK_K, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16),
+    b_pack: S.Tensor((B_PACK_K, B_PACK_N, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16),
+    bias: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WARP_SIZE
+    warp = tid // WARP_SIZE
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2
+
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    tile_row = block_row + warp_row * WARP_M
+    tile_col = block_col + warp_col * WARP_N
+
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(a_pack, A_PACK_RANGE_BYTES)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(b_pack, B_PACK_RANGE_BYTES)
+
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    a_smem = S.make_shared((NUM_WARPS, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((NUM_WARPS, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16)
+
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(A_PACK_K):
+        a_elem_offset = (((tile_row // WARP_M) * A_PACK_K + k_tile) * WARP_SIZE + lane) * 8
+        b_elem_offset = ((k_tile * B_PACK_N + (tile_col // WARP_N)) * WARP_SIZE + lane) * 8
+        a_byte_offset = S.convert(a_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+        b_byte_offset = S.convert(b_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+
+        a_frag_g = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, a_byte_offset, 0)
+        b_frag_g = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_byte_offset, 0)
+
+        a_frag_view = S.view(a_frag_g, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag_view = S.view(b_frag_g, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        for frag_half in S.range(2):
+            for frag_elem in S.range(4):
+                a_smem[warp, lane, frag_half * 4 + frag_elem] = a_frag_view[frag_half, frag_elem, 0]
+                b_smem[warp, lane, frag_half * 4 + frag_elem] = b_frag_view[frag_half, frag_elem, 0]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a0 = S.full((4, 1), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        a1 = S.full((4, 1), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        b0 = S.full((4, 1), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        b1 = S.full((4, 1), 0.0, S.bf16)
+        for frag_elem in S.range(4):
+            a0[frag_elem, 0] = a_smem[warp, lane, frag_elem]
+            a1[frag_elem, 0] = a_smem[warp, lane, 4 + frag_elem]
+            b0[frag_elem, 0] = b_smem[warp, lane, frag_elem]
+            b1[frag_elem, 0] = b_smem[warp, lane, 4 + frag_elem]
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a0, b0, acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a1, b1, acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    lane_col = lane % 32
+    lane_row_quad = lane // 32
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        out_col = tile_col + lane_col
+        out_row = tile_row + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * lane_row_quad + (acc_idx % 4)
+        value = acc[acc_idx] + S.convert(bias[out_col], S.f32)
+        y[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(value, S.bf16)
+

+def groupnorm_hardtanh_kernel(
+    y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    gn_weight: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    gn_bias: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    row = S.block_id(1)
+    group = S.block_id(0)
+    c0 = group * GROUP_SIZE + tid
+    c1 = c0 + 256
+
+    partial = S.make_shared((256,), S.f32)
+
+    sum_val = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+    sum_sq = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+
+    v0 = S.convert(y[row, c0], S.f32)
+    sum_val += v0
+    sum_sq += v0 * v0
+
+    v1 = S.convert(y[row, c1], S.f32)
+    sum_val += v1
+    sum_sq += v1 * v1
+
+    partial[tid] = sum_val
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    stride = 128
+    for _ in S.range(8):
+        if tid < stride:
+            partial[tid] = partial[tid] + partial[tid + stride]
+        S.syncthreads()
+        stride = stride >> 0x1
+
+    mean = partial[0] / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+    partial[tid] = sum_sq
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    stride = 128
+    for _ in S.range(8):
+        if tid < stride:
+            partial[tid] = partial[tid] + partial[tid + stride]
+        S.syncthreads()
+        stride = stride >> 0x1
+
+    mean_sq = partial[0] / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+    var = mean_sq - mean * mean
+    denom = S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))

 HARDTANH_MAX = 2.0
 EPS = 1e-05
 
+WARP_SIZE = 64
+NUM_WARPS = 4
+BLOCK_THREADS = WARP_SIZE * NUM_WARPS
+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+WARP_M = 32
+WARP_N = 32
+K_TILE = 16
+
+A_PACK_M = BATCH_SIZE // WARP_M
+A_PACK_K = IN_FEATURES // K_TILE
+B_PACK_K = IN_FEATURES // K_TILE
+B_PACK_N = OUT_FEATURES // WARP_N
+
+A_PACK_RANGE_BYTES = A_PACK_M * A_PACK_K * WARP_SIZE * 8 * 2
+B_PACK_RANGE_BYTES = B_PACK_K * B_PACK_N * WARP_SIZE * 8 * 2
+
+
+def _launch_gemm():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (BLOCK_THREADS, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _launch_post():
+    return ((NUM_GROUPS, BATCH_SIZE, 1), (256, 1, 1))
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_mfma_kernel(
+    a_pack: S.Tensor((A_PACK_M, A_PACK_K, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16),
+    b_pack: S.Tensor((B_PACK_K, B_PACK_N, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16),
+    bias: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WARP_SIZE
+    warp = tid // WARP_SIZE
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2
+
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    tile_row = block_row + warp_row * WARP_M
+    tile_col = block_col + warp_col * WARP_N
+
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(a_pack, A_PACK_RANGE_BYTES)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(b_pack, B_PACK_RANGE_BYTES)
+
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    a_smem = S.make_shared((NUM_WARPS, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((NUM_WARPS, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16)
+
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(A_PACK_K):
+        a_elem_offset = (((tile_row // WARP_M) * A_PACK_K + k_tile) * WARP_SIZE + lane) * 8
+        b_elem_offset = ((k_tile * B_PACK_N + (tile_col // WARP_N)) * WARP_SIZE + lane) * 8
+        a_byte_offset = S.convert(a_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+        b_byte_offset = S.convert(b_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+
+        a_frag_g = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, a_byte_offset, 0)
+        b_frag_g = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_byte_offset, 0)
+
+        a_frag_view = S.view(a_frag_g, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag_view = S.view(b_frag_g, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        for frag_half in S.range(2):
+            for frag_elem in S.range(4):
+                a_smem[warp, lane, frag_half * 4 + frag_elem] = a_frag_view[frag_half, frag_elem, 0]
+                b_smem[warp, lane, frag_half * 4 + frag_elem] = b_frag_view[frag_half, frag_elem, 0]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag_view[0], b_frag_view[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag_view[1], b_frag_view[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    lane_col = lane % 32
+    lane_row_quad = lane // 32
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        out_col = tile_col + lane_col
+        out_row = tile_row + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * lane_row_quad + (acc_idx % 4)
+        value = acc[acc_idx] + S.convert(bias[out_col], S.f32)
+        y[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(value, S.bf16)
+
+

+def groupnorm_hardtanh_kernel(
+    y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    gn_weight: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    gn_bias: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    row = S.block_id(1)
+    group = S.block_id(0)
+    c0 = group * GROUP_SIZE + tid
+    c1 = c0 + 256
+
+    partial = S.make_shared((256,), S.f32)
+
+    sum_val = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+    sum_sq = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+
+    v0 = S.convert(y[row, c0], S.f32)
+    sum_val += v0
+    sum_sq += v0 * v0
+
+    v1 = S.convert(y[row, c1], S.f32)
+    sum_val += v1
+    sum_sq += v1 * v1
+
+    partial[tid] = sum_val
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    stride = 128
+    for _ in S.range(8):
+        if tid < stride:
+            partial[tid] = partial[tid] + partial[tid + stride]
+        S.syncthreads()
+        stride = stride >> 0x1
+
+    mean = partial[0] / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+    partial[tid] = sum_sq
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    stride = 128
+    for _ in S.range(8):
+        if tid < stride:
+            partial[tid] = partial[tid] + partial[tid + stride]
+        S.syncthreads()
+        stride = stride >> 0x1
+
+    mean_sq = partial[0] / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+    var = mean_sq - mean * mean
+    denom = S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
+
+    n0 = (v0 - mean) / denom
+    n0 = n0 * S.convert(gn_weight[c0], S.f32) + S.convert(gn_bias[c0], S.f32)
+    if n0 < S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32):
+        n0 = S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32)
+    if n0 > S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32):
+        n0 = S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32)
+    y[row, c0] = S.convert(n0, S.bf16)
+
+    n1 = (v1 - mean) / denom
+    n1 = n1 * S.convert(gn_weight[c1], S.f32) + S.convert(gn_bias[c1], S.f32)
+    if n1 < S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32):
+        n1 = S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32)
+    if n1 > S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32):
+        n1 = S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32)
+    y[row, c1] = S.convert(n1, S.bf16)
+
+
+def _pack_a(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    xb = x.view(BATCH_SIZE // WARP_M, WARP_M, IN_FEATURES // K_TILE, K_TILE).permute(0, 2, 1, 3)
+    first = torch.cat((xb[:, :, :, 0:4], xb[:, :, :, 8:12]), dim=-1)
+    second = torch.cat((xb[:, :, :, 4:8], xb[:, :, :, 12:16]), dim=-1)
+    return torch.cat((first, second), dim=2).contiguous()
+
+
+def _pack_b(w: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    wb = w.view(IN_FEATURES // K_TILE, K_TILE, OUT_FEATURES // WARP_N, WARP_N).permute(0, 2, 1, 3)
+    groups = []
+    for g in range(WARP_N // 4):
+        cols = wb[:, :, :, g * 4 : (g + 1) * 4]
+        groups.append(torch.cat((cols[:, :, 0:8, :], cols[:, :, 8:16, :]), dim=1))
+    return torch.cat(groups, dim=2).contiguous()
+

+    def _refresh_static_buffers(self, device, dtype):
+        w = self.gemm.weight
+        b = self.gemm.bias
+        gw = self.group_norm.weight
+        gb = self.group_norm.bias
+
+        w_ptr = w.untyped_storage().data_ptr()
+        b_ptr = b.untyped_storage().data_ptr()
+        gw_ptr = gw.untyped_storage().data_ptr()
+        gb_ptr = gb.untyped_storage().data_ptr()
+
+        if (
+            self._b_pack is None
+            or self._cached_weight_ptr != w_ptr
+            or self._b_pack.device != device
+            or self._b_pack.dtype != dtype
+        ):
+            w_t = w.t().to(device=device, dtype=dtype).contiguous()

+        if self._y is None or self._y.device != device or self._y.dtype != dtype:

-                    v = S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32)
-                Y[i, c] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)
+def groupnorm_hardtanh_kernel(
+    y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    gn_weight: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    gn_bias: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    row = S.block_id(1)
+    group = S.block_id(0)
+    c0 = group * GROUP_SIZE + tid
+    c1 = c0 + 256
+
+    partial = S.make_shared((256,), S.f32)
+
+    sum_val = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+    sum_sq = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+
+    v0 = S.convert(y[row, c0], S.f32)
+    sum_val += v0
+    sum_sq += v0 * v0
+
+    v1 = S.convert(y[row, c1], S.f32)
+    sum_val += v1
+    sum_sq += v1 * v1
+
+    partial[tid] = sum_val
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    stride = 128
+    for _ in S.range(8):
+        if tid < stride:
+            partial[tid] = partial[tid] + partial[tid + stride]
+        S.syncthreads()
+        stride = stride >> 0x1
+
+    mean = partial[0] / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+    partial[tid] = sum_sq
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    stride = 128
+    for _ in S.range(8):
+        if tid < stride:
+            partial[tid] = partial[tid] + partial[tid + stride]
+        S.syncthreads()
+        stride = stride >> 0x1
+
+    mean_sq = partial[0] / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+    var = mean_sq - mean * mean
+    denom = S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
+
+    n0 = (v0 - mean) / denom
+    n0 = n0 * S.convert(gn_weight[c0], S.f32) + S.convert(gn_bias[c0], S.f32)
+    if n0 < S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32):
+        n0 = S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32)
+    if n0 > S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32):
+        n0 = S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32)
+    y[row, c0] = S.convert(n0, S.bf16)
+
+    n1 = (v1 - mean) / denom
+    n1 = n1 * S.convert(gn_weight[c1], S.f32) + S.convert(gn_bias[c1], S.f32)
+    if n1 < S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32):
+        n1 = S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32)
+    if n1 > S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32):
+        n1 = S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32)
+    y[row, c1] = S.convert(n1, S.bf16)
+
+
+def _pack_a(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    xb = x.view(BATCH_SIZE // WARP_M, WARP_M, IN_FEATURES // K_TILE, K_TILE).permute(0, 2, 1, 3)
+    first = torch.cat((xb[:, :, :, 0:4], xb[:, :, :, 8:12]), dim=-1)
+    second = torch.cat((xb[:, :, :, 4:8], xb[:, :, :, 12:16]), dim=-1)
+    return torch.cat((first, second), dim=2).contiguous()
+
+
+def _pack_b(w: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    wb = w.view(IN_FEATURES // K_TILE, K_TILE, OUT_FEATURES // WARP_N, WARP_N).permute(0, 2, 1, 3)
+    groups = []
+    for g in range(WARP_N // 4):
+        cols = wb[:, :, :, g * 4 : (g + 1) * 4]
+        groups.append(torch.cat((cols[:, :, 0:8, :], cols[:, :, 8:16, :]), dim=1))
+    return torch.cat(groups, dim=2).contiguous()
+

 HARDTANH_MAX = 2.0
 EPS = 1e-05
 
+WARP_SIZE = 64
+NUM_WARPS = 4
+BLOCK_THREADS = WARP_SIZE * NUM_WARPS
+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+WARP_M = 32
+WARP_N = 32
+K_TILE = 16
+
+A_PACK_M = BATCH_SIZE // WARP_M
+A_PACK_K = IN_FEATURES // K_TILE
+B_PACK_K = IN_FEATURES // K_TILE
+B_PACK_N = OUT_FEATURES // WARP_N
+
+A_PACK_RANGE_BYTES = A_PACK_M * A_PACK_K * WARP_SIZE * 8 * 2
+B_PACK_RANGE_BYTES = B_PACK_K * B_PACK_N * WARP_SIZE * 8 * 2
+
+
+def _launch_gemm():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (BLOCK_THREADS, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _launch_post():
+    return ((NUM_GROUPS, BATCH_SIZE, 1), (256, 1, 1))
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_mfma_kernel(
+    a_pack: S.Tensor((A_PACK_M, A_PACK_K, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16),
+    b_pack: S.Tensor((B_PACK_K, B_PACK_N, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16),
+    bias: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WARP_SIZE
+    warp = tid // WARP_SIZE
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2
+
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    tile_row = block_row + warp_row * WARP_M
+    tile_col = block_col + warp_col * WARP_N
+
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(a_pack, A_PACK_RANGE_BYTES)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(b_pack, B_PACK_RANGE_BYTES)
+
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    a_smem = S.make_shared((NUM_WARPS, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((NUM_WARPS, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16)
+
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(A_PACK_K):
+        a_elem_offset = (((tile_row // WARP_M) * A_PACK_K + k_tile) * WARP_SIZE + lane) * 8
+        b_elem_offset = ((k_tile * B_PACK_N + (tile_col // WARP_N)) * WARP_SIZE + lane) * 8
+        a_byte_offset = S.convert(a_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+        b_byte_offset = S.convert(b_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+
+        a_frag_g = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, a_byte_offset, 0)
+        b_frag_g = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_byte_offset, 0)
+
+        a_frag_view = S.view(a_frag_g, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag_view = S.view(b_frag_g, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        for frag_half in S.range(2):
+            for frag_elem in S.range(4):
+                a_smem[warp, lane, frag_half * 4 + frag_elem] = a_frag_view[frag_half, frag_elem, 0]
+                b_smem[warp, lane, frag_half * 4 + frag_elem] = b_frag_view[frag_half, frag_elem, 0]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag_view[0], b_frag_view[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag_view[1], b_frag_view[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    lane_col = lane % 32
+    lane_row_quad = lane // 32
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        out_col = tile_col + lane_col
+        out_row = tile_row + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * lane_row_quad + (acc_idx % 4)
+        value = acc[acc_idx] + S.convert(bias[out_col], S.f32)
+        y[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(value, S.bf16)
+
+

 HARDTANH_MAX = 2.0
 EPS = 1e-05
 
+WARP_SIZE = 64
+NUM_WARPS = 4
+BLOCK_THREADS = WARP_SIZE * NUM_WARPS
+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+WARP_M = 32
+WARP_N = 32
+K_TILE = 16
+
+A_PACK_M = BATCH_SIZE // WARP_M
+A_PACK_K = IN_FEATURES // K_TILE
+B_PACK_K = IN_FEATURES // K_TILE
+B_PACK_N = OUT_FEATURES // WARP_N
+
+A_PACK_RANGE_BYTES = A_PACK_M * A_PACK_K * WARP_SIZE * 8 * 2
+B_PACK_RANGE_BYTES = B_PACK_K * B_PACK_N * WARP_SIZE * 8 * 2
+
+
+def _launch_gemm():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (BLOCK_THREADS, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _launch_post():
+    return ((NUM_GROUPS, BATCH_SIZE, 1), (256, 1, 1))

+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_mfma_kernel(
+    a_pack: S.Tensor((A_PACK_M, A_PACK_K, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16),
+    b_pack: S.Tensor((B_PACK_K, B_PACK_N, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16),
+    bias: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WARP_SIZE
+    warp = tid // WARP_SIZE
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2
+
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    tile_row = block_row + warp_row * WARP_M
+    tile_col = block_col + warp_col * WARP_N
+
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(a_pack, A_PACK_RANGE_BYTES)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(b_pack, B_PACK_RANGE_BYTES)
+
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    a_smem = S.make_shared((NUM_WARPS, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((NUM_WARPS, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16)
+
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(A_PACK_K):
+        a_elem_offset = (((tile_row // WARP_M) * A_PACK_K + k_tile) * WARP_SIZE + lane) * 8
+        b_elem_offset = ((k_tile * B_PACK_N + (tile_col // WARP_N)) * WARP_SIZE + lane) * 8
+        a_byte_offset = S.convert(a_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+        b_byte_offset = S.convert(b_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+
+        a_frag_g = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, a_byte_offset, 0)
+        b_frag_g = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_byte_offset, 0)
+
+        a_frag_view = S.view(a_frag_g, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag_view = S.view(b_frag_g, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        for frag_half in S.range(2):
+            for frag_elem in S.range(4):
+                a_smem[warp, lane, frag_half * 4 + frag_elem] = a_frag_view[frag_half, frag_elem, 0]
+                b_smem[warp, lane, frag_half * 4 + frag_elem] = b_frag_view[frag_half, frag_elem, 0]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag_view[0], b_frag_view[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag_view[1], b_frag_view[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    lane_col = lane % 32
+    lane_row_quad = lane // 32
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        out_col = tile_col + lane_col
+        out_row = tile_row + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * lane_row_quad + (acc_idx % 4)
+        value = acc[acc_idx] + S.convert(bias[out_col], S.f32)
+        y[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(value, S.bf16)
+

+def groupnorm_hardtanh_kernel(
+    y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    gn_weight: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    gn_bias: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    row = S.block_id(1)
+    group = S.block_id(0)
+    c0 = group * GROUP_SIZE + tid
+    c1 = c0 + 256
+
+    partial = S.make_shared((256,), S.f32)
+
+    sum_val = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+    sum_sq = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+
+    v0 = S.convert(y[row, c0], S.f32)
+    sum_val += v0
+    sum_sq += v0 * v0
+
+    v1 = S.convert(y[row, c1], S.f32)
+    sum_val += v1
+    sum_sq += v1 * v1
+
+    partial[tid] = sum_val
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    stride = 128
+    for _ in S.range(8):
+        if tid < stride:
+            partial[tid] = partial[tid] + partial[tid + stride]
+        S.syncthreads()
+        stride = stride >> 0x1
+
+    mean = partial[0] / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+    partial[tid] = sum_sq
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    stride = 128
+    for _ in S.range(8):
+        if tid < stride:
+            partial[tid] = partial[tid] + partial[tid + stride]
+        S.syncthreads()
+        stride = stride >> 0x1
+
+    mean_sq = partial[0] / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+    var = mean_sq - mean * mean
+    denom = S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
+
+    n0 = (v0 - mean) / denom
+    n0 = n0 * S.convert(gn_weight[c0], S.f32) + S.convert(gn_bias[c0], S.f32)
+    if n0 < S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32):
+        n0 = S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32)
+    if n0 > S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32):
+        n0 = S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32)
+    y[row, c0] = S.convert(n0, S.bf16)
+
+    n1 = (v1 - mean) / denom
+    n1 = n1 * S.convert(gn_weight[c1], S.f32) + S.convert(gn_bias[c1], S.f32)
+    if n1 < S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32):
+        n1 = S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32)
+    if n1 > S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32):
+        n1 = S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32)
+    y[row, c1] = S.convert(n1, S.bf16)
+
+
+def _pack_a(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    xb = x.view(BATCH_SIZE // WARP_M, WARP_M, IN_FEATURES // K_TILE, K_TILE).permute(0, 2, 1, 3)
+    first = torch.cat((xb[:, :, :, 0:4], xb[:, :, :, 8:12]), dim=-1)
+    second = torch.cat((xb[:, :, :, 4:8], xb[:, :, :, 12:16]), dim=-1)
+    return torch.cat((first, second), dim=2).contiguous()
+
+
+def _pack_b(w: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    wb = w.view(IN_FEATURES // K_TILE, K_TILE, OUT_FEATURES // WARP_N, WARP_N).permute(0, 2, 1, 3)
+    groups = []
+    for g in range(WARP_N // 4):
+        cols = wb[:, :, :, g * 4 : (g + 1) * 4]
+        groups.append(torch.cat((cols[:, :, 0:8, :], cols[:, :, 8:16, :]), dim=1))
+    return torch.cat(groups, dim=2).contiguous()

 HARDTANH_MAX = 2.0
 EPS = 1e-05
 
+WARP_SIZE = 64
+NUM_WARPS = 4
+BLOCK_THREADS = WARP_SIZE * NUM_WARPS
+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+WARP_M = 32
+WARP_N = 32
+K_TILE = 16
+
+A_PACK_M = BATCH_SIZE // WARP_M
+A_PACK_K = IN_FEATURES // K_TILE
+B_PACK_K = IN_FEATURES // K_TILE
+B_PACK_N = OUT_FEATURES // WARP_N
+
+A_PACK_RANGE_BYTES = A_PACK_M * A_PACK_K * WARP_SIZE * 8 * 2
+B_PACK_RANGE_BYTES = B_PACK_K * B_PACK_N * WARP_SIZE * 8 * 2
+
+
+def _launch_gemm():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (BLOCK_THREADS, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _launch_post():
+    return ((NUM_GROUPS, BATCH_SIZE, 1), (256, 1, 1))
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_mfma_kernel(
+    a_pack: S.Tensor((A_PACK_M, A_PACK_K, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16),
+    b_pack: S.Tensor((B_PACK_K, B_PACK_N, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16),
+    bias: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WARP_SIZE
+    warp = tid // WARP_SIZE
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2
+
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    tile_row = block_row + warp_row * WARP_M
+    tile_col = block_col + warp_col * WARP_N
+
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(a_pack, A_PACK_RANGE_BYTES)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(b_pack, B_PACK_RANGE_BYTES)
+
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    a_smem = S.make_shared((NUM_WARPS, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((NUM_WARPS, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16)
+
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(A_PACK_K):
+        a_elem_offset = (((tile_row // WARP_M) * A_PACK_K + k_tile) * WARP_SIZE + lane) * 8
+        b_elem_offset = ((k_tile * B_PACK_N + (tile_col // WARP_N)) * WARP_SIZE + lane) * 8
+        a_byte_offset = S.convert(a_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+        b_byte_offset = S.convert(b_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+
+        a_frag_g = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, a_byte_offset, 0)
+        b_frag_g = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_byte_offset, 0)
+
+        a_frag_view = S.view(a_frag_g, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag_view = S.view(b_frag_g, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        for frag_half in S.range(2):
+            for frag_elem in S.range(4):
+                a_smem[warp, lane, frag_half * 4 + frag_elem] = a_frag_view[frag_half, frag_elem, 0]
+                b_smem[warp, lane, frag_half * 4 + frag_elem] = b_frag_view[frag_half, frag_elem, 0]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag_view[0], b_frag_view[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag_view[1], b_frag_view[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    lane_col = lane % 32
+    lane_row_quad = lane // 32
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        out_col = tile_col + lane_col
+        out_row = tile_row + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * lane_row_quad + (acc_idx % 4)
+        value = acc[acc_idx] + S.convert(bias[out_col], S.f32)
+        y[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(value, S.bf16)
+
+

+def groupnorm_hardtanh_kernel(
+    y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    gn_weight: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    gn_bias: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    row = S.block_id(1)
+    group = S.block_id(0)
+    c0 = group * GROUP_SIZE + tid
+    c1 = c0 + 256
+
+    partial = S.make_shared((256,), S.f32)
+
+    sum_val = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+    sum_sq = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+
+    v0 = S.convert(y[row, c0], S.f32)
+    sum_val += v0
+    sum_sq += v0 * v0
+
+    v1 = S.convert(y[row, c1], S.f32)
+    sum_val += v1
+    sum_sq += v1 * v1
+
+    partial[tid] = sum_val
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    stride = 128
+    for _ in S.range(8):
+        if tid < stride:
+            partial[tid] = partial[tid] + partial[tid + stride]
+        S.syncthreads()
+        stride = stride >> 0x1
+
+    mean = partial[0] / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+    partial[tid] = sum_sq
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    stride = 128
+    for _ in S.range(8):
+        if tid < stride:
+            partial[tid] = partial[tid] + partial[tid + stride]
+        S.syncthreads()
+        stride = stride >> 0x1
+
+    mean_sq = partial[0] / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+    var = mean_sq - mean * mean
+    denom = S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
+
+    n0 = (v0 - mean) / denom
+    n0 = n0 * S.convert(gn_weight[c0], S.f32) + S.convert(gn_bias[c0], S.f32)
+    if n0 < S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32):
+        n0 = S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32)
+    if n0 > S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32):
+        n0 = S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32)
+    y[row, c0] = S.convert(n0, S.bf16)
+
+    n1 = (v1 - mean) / denom
+    n1 = n1 * S.convert(gn_weight[c1], S.f32) + S.convert(gn_bias[c1], S.f32)
+    if n1 < S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32):
+        n1 = S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32)
+    if n1 > S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32):
+        n1 = S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32)
+    y[row, c1] = S.convert(n1, S.bf16)
+
+
+def _pack_a(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    xb = x.view(BATCH_SIZE // WARP_M, WARP_M, IN_FEATURES // K_TILE, K_TILE).permute(0, 2, 1, 3)
+    first = torch.cat((xb[:, :, :, 0:4], xb[:, :, :, 8:12]), dim=-1)
+    second = torch.cat((xb[:, :, :, 4:8], xb[:, :, :, 12:16]), dim=-1)
+    return torch.cat((first, second), dim=2).contiguous()
+
+
+def _pack_b(w: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    wb = w.view(IN_FEATURES // K_TILE, K_TILE, OUT_FEATURES // WARP_N, WARP_N).permute(0, 2, 1, 3)
+    groups = []
+    for g in range(WARP_N // 4):
+        cols = wb[:, :, :, g * 4 : (g + 1) * 4]
+        groups.append(torch.cat((cols[:, :, 0:8, :], cols[:, :, 8:16, :]), dim=1))
+    return torch.cat(groups, dim=2).contiguous()
+

+    def _refresh_static_buffers(self, device, dtype):
+        w = self.gemm.weight
+        b = self.gemm.bias
+        gw = self.group_norm.weight
+        gb = self.group_norm.bias
+
+        w_ptr = w.untyped_storage().data_ptr()
+        b_ptr = b.untyped_storage().data_ptr()
+        gw_ptr = gw.untyped_storage().data_ptr()
+        gb_ptr = gb.untyped_storage().data_ptr()
+
+        if (
+            self._b_pack is None
+            or self._cached_weight_ptr != w_ptr
+            or self._b_pack.device != device
+            or self._b_pack.dtype != dtype
+        ):
+            w_t = w.t().to(device=device, dtype=dtype).contiguous()
+            self._b_pack = _pack_b(w_t)
+            self._cached_weight_ptr = w_ptr
+
+        if (
+            self._bias is None
+            or self._cached_bias_ptr != b_ptr

+            or self._bias.dtype != dtype

+            self._cached_bias_ptr = b_ptr
+
+        if (
+            self._gn_weight is None
+            or self._cached_gn_weight_ptr != gw_ptr
+            or self._gn_weight.device != device
+            or self._gn_weight.dtype != dtype

+            self._gn_weight = gw.to(device=device, dtype=dtype).contiguous()

+
+        if (
+            self._gn_bias is None
+            or self._cached_gn_bias_ptr != gb_ptr
+            or self._gn_bias.device != device

+            self._cached_gn_bias_ptr = gb_ptr
+
+        if self._y is None or self._y.device != device or self._y.dtype != dtype:
+            self._y = torch.empty((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), device=device, dtype=dtype)

The current mismatch is most likely the B operand pack, not the post-op math. There’s a concrete dimensional bug in that packer, and I’m fixing it before rerunning the exact evaluation command.

-                    v = S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32)
-                Y[i, c] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)
+def groupnorm_hardtanh_kernel(
+    y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    gn_weight: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    gn_bias: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    row = S.block_id(1)
+    group = S.block_id(0)
+    c0 = group * GROUP_SIZE + tid
+    c1 = c0 + 256
+
+    partial = S.make_shared((256,), S.f32)
+
+    sum_val = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+    sum_sq = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+
+    v0 = S.convert(y[row, c0], S.f32)
+    sum_val += v0
+    sum_sq += v0 * v0
+
+    v1 = S.convert(y[row, c1], S.f32)
+    sum_val += v1
+    sum_sq += v1 * v1
+
+    partial[tid] = sum_val
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    stride = 128
+    for _ in S.range(8):
+        if tid < stride:
+            partial[tid] = partial[tid] + partial[tid + stride]
+        S.syncthreads()
+        stride = stride >> 0x1
+
+    mean = partial[0] / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+    partial[tid] = sum_sq
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    stride = 128
+    for _ in S.range(8):
+        if tid < stride:
+            partial[tid] = partial[tid] + partial[tid + stride]
+        S.syncthreads()
+        stride = stride >> 0x1
+
+    mean_sq = partial[0] / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+    var = mean_sq - mean * mean
+    denom = S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
+
+    n0 = (v0 - mean) / denom
+    n0 = n0 * S.convert(gn_weight[c0], S.f32) + S.convert(gn_bias[c0], S.f32)
+    if n0 < S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32):
+        n0 = S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32)
+    if n0 > S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32):
+        n0 = S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32)
+    y[row, c0] = S.convert(n0, S.bf16)
+
+    n1 = (v1 - mean) / denom
+    n1 = n1 * S.convert(gn_weight[c1], S.f32) + S.convert(gn_bias[c1], S.f32)
+    if n1 < S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32):
+        n1 = S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32)
+    if n1 > S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32):
+        n1 = S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32)
+    y[row, c1] = S.convert(n1, S.bf16)
+
+
+def _pack_a(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    xb = x.view(BATCH_SIZE // WARP_M, WARP_M, IN_FEATURES // K_TILE, K_TILE).permute(0, 2, 1, 3)
+    first = torch.cat((xb[:, :, :, 0:4], xb[:, :, :, 8:12]), dim=-1)
+    second = torch.cat((xb[:, :, :, 4:8], xb[:, :, :, 12:16]), dim=-1)
+    return torch.cat((first, second), dim=2).contiguous()
+
+
+def _pack_b(w: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    wb = w.view(IN_FEATURES // K_TILE, K_TILE, OUT_FEATURES // WARP_N, WARP_N).permute(0, 2, 1, 3)
+    groups = []
+    for g in range(WARP_N // 4):
+        cols = wb[:, :, :, g * 4 : (g + 1) * 4]
+        groups.append(torch.cat((cols[:, :, 0:8, :], cols[:, :, 8:16, :]), dim=-1))
+    return torch.cat(groups, dim=2).contiguous()
+

 HARDTANH_MAX = 2.0
 EPS = 1e-05
 
+WARP_SIZE = 64
+NUM_WARPS = 4
+BLOCK_THREADS = WARP_SIZE * NUM_WARPS
+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+WARP_M = 32
+WARP_N = 32
+K_TILE = 16
+
+A_PACK_M = BATCH_SIZE // WARP_M
+A_PACK_K = IN_FEATURES // K_TILE
+B_PACK_K = IN_FEATURES // K_TILE
+B_PACK_N = OUT_FEATURES // WARP_N
+
+A_PACK_RANGE_BYTES = A_PACK_M * A_PACK_K * WARP_SIZE * 8 * 2
+B_PACK_RANGE_BYTES = B_PACK_K * B_PACK_N * WARP_SIZE * 8 * 2
+
+
+def _launch_gemm():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (BLOCK_THREADS, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _launch_post():
+    return ((NUM_GROUPS, BATCH_SIZE, 1), (256, 1, 1))
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_mfma_kernel(
+    a_pack: S.Tensor((A_PACK_M, A_PACK_K, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16),
+    b_pack: S.Tensor((B_PACK_K, B_PACK_N, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16),
+    bias: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WARP_SIZE
+    warp = tid // WARP_SIZE
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2
+
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    tile_row = block_row + warp_row * WARP_M
+    tile_col = block_col + warp_col * WARP_N
+
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(a_pack, A_PACK_RANGE_BYTES)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(b_pack, B_PACK_RANGE_BYTES)
+
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    a_smem = S.make_shared((NUM_WARPS, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((NUM_WARPS, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16)
+
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(A_PACK_K):
+        a_elem_offset = (((tile_row // WARP_M) * A_PACK_K + k_tile) * WARP_SIZE + lane) * 8
+        b_elem_offset = ((k_tile * B_PACK_N + (tile_col // WARP_N)) * WARP_SIZE + lane) * 8
+        a_byte_offset = S.convert(a_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+        b_byte_offset = S.convert(b_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+
+        a_frag_g = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, a_byte_offset, 0)
+        b_frag_g = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_byte_offset, 0)
+
+        a_frag_view = S.view(a_frag_g, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag_view = S.view(b_frag_g, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        for frag_half in S.range(2):
+            for frag_elem in S.range(4):
+                a_smem[warp, lane, frag_half * 4 + frag_elem] = a_frag_view[frag_half, frag_elem, 0]
+                b_smem[warp, lane, frag_half * 4 + frag_elem] = b_frag_view[frag_half, frag_elem, 0]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag_view[0], b_frag_view[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag_view[1], b_frag_view[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    lane_col = lane % 32
+    lane_row_quad = lane // 32
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        out_col = tile_col + lane_col
+        out_row = tile_row + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * lane_row_quad + (acc_idx % 4)
+        value = acc[acc_idx] + S.convert(bias[out_col], S.f32)
+        y[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(value, S.bf16)
+

 HARDTANH_MAX = 2.0
 EPS = 1e-05
 
+WARP_SIZE = 64
+NUM_WARPS = 4
+BLOCK_THREADS = WARP_SIZE * NUM_WARPS
+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+WARP_M = 32
+WARP_N = 32
+K_TILE = 16
+
+A_PACK_M = BATCH_SIZE // WARP_M
+A_PACK_K = IN_FEATURES // K_TILE
+B_PACK_K = IN_FEATURES // K_TILE
+B_PACK_N = OUT_FEATURES // WARP_N
+
+A_PACK_RANGE_BYTES = A_PACK_M * A_PACK_K * WARP_SIZE * 8 * 2
+B_PACK_RANGE_BYTES = B_PACK_K * B_PACK_N * WARP_SIZE * 8 * 2
+
+
+def _launch_gemm():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (BLOCK_THREADS, 1, 1))

+
+def _launch_post():
+    return ((NUM_GROUPS, BATCH_SIZE, 1), (256, 1, 1))

+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_mfma_kernel(
+    a_pack: S.Tensor((A_PACK_M, A_PACK_K, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16),
+    b_pack: S.Tensor((B_PACK_K, B_PACK_N, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16),
+    bias: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WARP_SIZE
+    warp = tid // WARP_SIZE
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2
+
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    tile_row = block_row + warp_row * WARP_M
+    tile_col = block_col + warp_col * WARP_N
+
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(a_pack, A_PACK_RANGE_BYTES)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(b_pack, B_PACK_RANGE_BYTES)
+
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    a_smem = S.make_shared((NUM_WARPS, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((NUM_WARPS, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16)
+
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(A_PACK_K):
+        a_elem_offset = (((tile_row // WARP_M) * A_PACK_K + k_tile) * WARP_SIZE + lane) * 8
+        b_elem_offset = ((k_tile * B_PACK_N + (tile_col // WARP_N)) * WARP_SIZE + lane) * 8
+        a_byte_offset = S.convert(a_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+        b_byte_offset = S.convert(b_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+
+        a_frag_g = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, a_byte_offset, 0)
+        b_frag_g = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_byte_offset, 0)
+
+        a_frag_view = S.view(a_frag_g, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag_view = S.view(b_frag_g, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        for frag_half in S.range(2):
+            for frag_elem in S.range(4):
+                a_smem[warp, lane, frag_half * 4 + frag_elem] = a_frag_view[frag_half, frag_elem, 0]
+                b_smem[warp, lane, frag_half * 4 + frag_elem] = b_frag_view[frag_half, frag_elem, 0]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag_view[0], b_frag_view[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag_view[1], b_frag_view[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    lane_col = lane % 32
+    lane_row_quad = lane // 32
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        out_col = tile_col + lane_col
+        out_row = tile_row + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * lane_row_quad + (acc_idx % 4)
+        value = acc[acc_idx] + S.convert(bias[out_col], S.f32)
+        y[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(value, S.bf16)
+

+def groupnorm_hardtanh_kernel(
+    y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    gn_weight: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    gn_bias: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    row = S.block_id(1)
+    group = S.block_id(0)
+    c0 = group * GROUP_SIZE + tid
+    c1 = c0 + 256
+
+    partial = S.make_shared((256,), S.f32)
+
+    sum_val = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+    sum_sq = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+
+    v0 = S.convert(y[row, c0], S.f32)
+    sum_val += v0
+    sum_sq += v0 * v0
+
+    v1 = S.convert(y[row, c1], S.f32)
+    sum_val += v1
+    sum_sq += v1 * v1
+
+    partial[tid] = sum_val
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    stride = 128
+    for _ in S.range(8):
+        if tid < stride:
+            partial[tid] = partial[tid] + partial[tid + stride]
+        S.syncthreads()
+        stride = stride >> 0x1
+
+    mean = partial[0] / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+    partial[tid] = sum_sq
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    stride = 128
+    for _ in S.range(8):
+        if tid < stride:
+            partial[tid] = partial[tid] + partial[tid + stride]
+        S.syncthreads()
+        stride = stride >> 0x1
+
+    mean_sq = partial[0] / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+    var = mean_sq - mean * mean
+    denom = S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
+
+    n0 = (v0 - mean) / denom
+    n0 = n0 * S.convert(gn_weight[c0], S.f32) + S.convert(gn_bias[c0], S.f32)
+    if n0 < S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32):
+        n0 = S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32)
+    if n0 > S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32):
+        n0 = S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32)
+    y[row, c0] = S.convert(n0, S.bf16)
+
+    n1 = (v1 - mean) / denom
+    n1 = n1 * S.convert(gn_weight[c1], S.f32) + S.convert(gn_bias[c1], S.f32)
+    if n1 < S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32):
+        n1 = S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32)
+    if n1 > S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32):
+        n1 = S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32)
+    y[row, c1] = S.convert(n1, S.bf16)
+
+
+def _pack_a(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    xb = x.view(BATCH_SIZE // WARP_M, WARP_M, IN_FEATURES // K_TILE, K_TILE).permute(0, 2, 1, 3)
+    first = torch.cat((xb[:, :, :, 0:4], xb[:, :, :, 8:12]), dim=-1)
+    second = torch.cat((xb[:, :, :, 4:8], xb[:, :, :, 12:16]), dim=-1)
+    return torch.cat((first, second), dim=2).contiguous()
+
+
+def _pack_b(w: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    wb = w.view(IN_FEATURES // K_TILE, K_TILE, OUT_FEATURES // WARP_N, WARP_N).permute(0, 2, 1, 3)
+    groups = []
+    for g in range(WARP_N // 4):
+        cols = wb[:, :, :, g * 4 : (g + 1) * 4]
+        groups.append(torch.cat((cols[:, :, 0:8, :], cols[:, :, 8:16, :]), dim=-1))
+    return torch.cat(groups, dim=2).contiguous()
+

+def groupnorm_hardtanh_kernel(
+    y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    gn_weight: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    gn_bias: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    row = S.block_id(1)
+    group = S.block_id(0)
+    c0 = group * GROUP_SIZE + tid
+    c1 = c0 + 256
+
+    partial = S.make_shared((256,), S.f32)
+
+    sum_val = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+    sum_sq = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+
+    v0 = S.convert(y[row, c0], S.f32)
+    sum_val += v0
+    sum_sq += v0 * v0
+
+    v1 = S.convert(y[row, c1], S.f32)
+    sum_val += v1
+    sum_sq += v1 * v1
+
+    partial[tid] = sum_val
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    stride = 128
+    for _ in S.range(8):
+        if tid < stride:
+            partial[tid] = partial[tid] + partial[tid + stride]
+        S.syncthreads()
+        stride = stride >> 0x1
+
+    mean = partial[0] / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+    partial[tid] = sum_sq
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    stride = 128
+    for _ in S.range(8):
+        if tid < stride:
+            partial[tid] = partial[tid] + partial[tid + stride]
+        S.syncthreads()
+        stride = stride >> 0x1
+
+    mean_sq = partial[0] / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+    var = mean_sq - mean * mean
+    denom = S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
+
+    n0 = (v0 - mean) / denom
+    n0 = n0 * S.convert(gn_weight[c0], S.f32) + S.convert(gn_bias[c0], S.f32)
+    if n0 < S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32):
+        n0 = S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32)
+    if n0 > S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32):
+        n0 = S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32)
+    y[row, c0] = S.convert(n0, S.bf16)
+
+    n1 = (v1 - mean) / denom
+    n1 = n1 * S.convert(gn_weight[c1], S.f32) + S.convert(gn_bias[c1], S.f32)
+    if n1 < S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32):
+        n1 = S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32)
+    if n1 > S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32):
+        n1 = S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32)
+    y[row, c1] = S.convert(n1, S.bf16)
+
+
+def _pack_a(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    xb = x.view(BATCH_SIZE // WARP_M, WARP_M, IN_FEATURES // K_TILE, K_TILE).permute(0, 2, 1, 3)
+    first = torch.cat((xb[:, :, :, 0:4], xb[:, :, :, 8:12]), dim=-1)
+    second = torch.cat((xb[:, :, :, 4:8], xb[:, :, :, 12:16]), dim=-1)
+    return torch.cat((first, second), dim=2).contiguous()
+
+
+def _pack_b(w: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    wb = w.view(IN_FEATURES // K_TILE, K_TILE, OUT_FEATURES // WARP_N, WARP_N).permute(0, 2, 1, 3)
+    groups = []
+    for g in range(WARP_N // 4):
+        cols = wb[:, :, :, g * 4 : (g + 1) * 4]
+        groups.append(torch.cat((cols[:, :, 0:8, :], cols[:, :, 8:16, :]), dim=-1))
+    return torch.cat(groups, dim=2).contiguous()
+

 HARDTANH_MAX = 2.0
 EPS = 1e-05
 
+WARP_SIZE = 64
+NUM_WARPS = 4
+BLOCK_THREADS = WARP_SIZE * NUM_WARPS
+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+WARP_M = 32
+WARP_N = 32
+K_TILE = 16
+
+A_PACK_M = BATCH_SIZE // WARP_M
+A_PACK_K = IN_FEATURES // K_TILE
+B_PACK_K = IN_FEATURES // K_TILE
+B_PACK_N = OUT_FEATURES // WARP_N
+
+A_PACK_RANGE_BYTES = A_PACK_M * A_PACK_K * WARP_SIZE * 8 * 2
+B_PACK_RANGE_BYTES = B_PACK_K * B_PACK_N * WARP_SIZE * 8 * 2
+
+
+def _launch_gemm():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (BLOCK_THREADS, 1, 1))

+def _launch_post():
+    return ((NUM_GROUPS, BATCH_SIZE, 1), (256, 1, 1))

+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_mfma_kernel(
+    a_pack: S.Tensor((A_PACK_M, A_PACK_K, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16),
+    b_pack: S.Tensor((B_PACK_K, B_PACK_N, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16),
+    bias: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WARP_SIZE
+    warp = tid // WARP_SIZE
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2
+
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    tile_row = block_row + warp_row * WARP_M
+    tile_col = block_col + warp_col * WARP_N
+
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(a_pack, A_PACK_RANGE_BYTES)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(b_pack, B_PACK_RANGE_BYTES)
+
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    a_smem = S.make_shared((NUM_WARPS, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((NUM_WARPS, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16)
+
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(A_PACK_K):
+        a_elem_offset = (((tile_row // WARP_M) * A_PACK_K + k_tile) * WARP_SIZE + lane) * 8
+        b_elem_offset = ((k_tile * B_PACK_N + (tile_col // WARP_N)) * WARP_SIZE + lane) * 8

+        b_frag_g = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_byte_offset, 0)
+
+        a_frag_view = S.view(a_frag_g, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))

+        S.syncthreads()

+def groupnorm_hardtanh_kernel(
+    y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),

+    sum_sq += v1 * v1
+
+    partial[tid] = sum_val
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    stride = 128
+    for _ in S.range(8):
+        if tid < stride:
+            partial[tid] = partial[tid] + partial[tid + stride]
+        S.syncthreads()
+        stride = stride >> 0x1
+
+    mean = partial[0] / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+    partial[tid] = sum_sq
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    stride = 128
+    for _ in S.range(8):
+        if tid < stride:
+            partial[tid] = partial[tid] + partial[tid + stride]
+        S.syncthreads()
+        stride = stride >> 0x1
+
+    mean_sq = partial[0] / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+    var = mean_sq - mean * mean
+    denom = S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
+
+    n0 = (v0 - mean) / denom
+    n0 = n0 * S.convert(gn_weight[c0], S.f32) + S.convert(gn_bias[c0], S.f32)
+    if n0 < S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32):
+        n0 = S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32)
+    if n0 > S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32):
+        n0 = S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32)
+    y[row, c0] = S.convert(n0, S.bf16)
+
+    n1 = (v1 - mean) / denom
+    n1 = n1 * S.convert(gn_weight[c1], S.f32) + S.convert(gn_bias[c1], S.f32)
+    if n1 < S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32):
+        n1 = S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32)
+    if n1 > S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32):
+        n1 = S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32)
+    y[row, c1] = S.convert(n1, S.bf16)
+
+
+def _pack_a(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    xb = x.view(BATCH_SIZE // WARP_M, WARP_M, IN_FEATURES // K_TILE, K_TILE).permute(0, 2, 1, 3)
+    first = torch.cat((xb[:, :, :, 0:4], xb[:, :, :, 8:12]), dim=-1)
+    second = torch.cat((xb[:, :, :, 4:8], xb[:, :, :, 12:16]), dim=-1)
+    return torch.cat((first, second), dim=2).contiguous()
+
+
+def _pack_b(w: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    wb = w.view(IN_FEATURES // K_TILE, K_TILE, OUT_FEATURES // WARP_N, WARP_N).permute(0, 2, 1, 3)
+    groups = []
+    for g in range(WARP_N // 4):
+        cols = wb[:, :, :, g * 4 : (g + 1) * 4]
+        groups.append(torch.cat((cols[:, :, 0:8, :], cols[:, :, 8:16, :]), dim=-1))
+    return torch.cat(groups, dim=2).contiguous()
+

+def gemm_mfma_kernel(
+    a_pack: S.Tensor((A_PACK_M, A_PACK_K, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16),
+    b_pack: S.Tensor((B_PACK_K, B_PACK_N, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16),
+    bias: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WARP_SIZE
+    warp = tid // WARP_SIZE
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2
+
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    tile_row = block_row + warp_row * WARP_M
+    tile_col = block_col + warp_col * WARP_N
+
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(a_pack, A_PACK_RANGE_BYTES)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(b_pack, B_PACK_RANGE_BYTES)
+
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    a_smem = S.make_shared((NUM_WARPS, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((NUM_WARPS, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16)
+
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(A_PACK_K):
+        a_elem_offset = (((tile_row // WARP_M) * A_PACK_K + k_tile) * WARP_SIZE + lane) * 8
+        b_elem_offset = ((k_tile * B_PACK_N + (tile_col // WARP_N)) * WARP_SIZE + lane) * 8
+        a_byte_offset = S.convert(a_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+        b_byte_offset = S.convert(b_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+
+        a_frag_g = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, a_byte_offset, 0)
+        b_frag_g = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_byte_offset, 0)
+
+        a_frag_view = S.view(a_frag_g, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag_view = S.view(b_frag_g, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        for frag_half in S.range(2):
+            for frag_elem in S.range(4):
+                a_smem[warp, lane, frag_half * 4 + frag_elem] = a_frag_view[frag_half, frag_elem, 0]
+                b_smem[warp, lane, frag_half * 4 + frag_elem] = b_frag_view[frag_half, frag_elem, 0]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag_view[0], b_frag_view[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag_view[1], b_frag_view[1], acc)

+        S.syncthreads()

+def _launch_gemm():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (BLOCK_THREADS, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _launch_post():
+    return ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_mfma_kernel(
+    a_pack: S.Tensor((A_PACK_M, A_PACK_K, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16),
+    b_pack: S.Tensor((B_PACK_K, B_PACK_N, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16),
+    bias: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WARP_SIZE
+    warp = tid // WARP_SIZE
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2
+
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    tile_row = block_row + warp_row * WARP_M
+    tile_col = block_col + warp_col * WARP_N
+
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(a_pack, A_PACK_RANGE_BYTES)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(b_pack, B_PACK_RANGE_BYTES)
+
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    a_smem = S.make_shared((NUM_WARPS, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((NUM_WARPS, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16)
+
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(A_PACK_K):
+        a_elem_offset = (((tile_row // WARP_M) * A_PACK_K + k_tile) * WARP_SIZE + lane) * 8
+        b_elem_offset = ((k_tile * B_PACK_N + (tile_col // WARP_N)) * WARP_SIZE + lane) * 8
+        a_byte_offset = S.convert(a_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+        b_byte_offset = S.convert(b_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+
+        a_frag_g = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, a_byte_offset, 0)
+        b_frag_g = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_byte_offset, 0)
+
+        a_frag_view = S.view(a_frag_g, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag_view = S.view(b_frag_g, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        for frag_half in S.range(2):
+            for frag_elem in S.range(4):
+                a_smem[warp, lane, frag_half * 4 + frag_elem] = a_frag_view[frag_half, frag_elem, 0]
+                b_smem[warp, lane, frag_half * 4 + frag_elem] = b_frag_view[frag_half, frag_elem, 0]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag_view[0], b_frag_view[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag_view[1], b_frag_view[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    lane_col = lane % 32
+    lane_row_quad = lane // 32
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        out_col = tile_col + lane_col
+        out_row = tile_row + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * lane_row_quad + (acc_idx % 4)
+        value = acc[acc_idx] + S.convert(bias[out_col], S.f32)
+        y[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(value, S.bf16)
+
+

+def _pack_a(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:

+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_mfma_kernel(
+    a_pack: S.Tensor((A_PACK_M, A_PACK_K, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16),
+    b_pack: S.Tensor((B_PACK_K, B_PACK_N, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16),
+    bias: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WARP_SIZE
+    warp = tid // WARP_SIZE
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2
+
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    tile_row = block_row + warp_row * WARP_M
+    tile_col = block_col + warp_col * WARP_N
+
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(a_pack, A_PACK_RANGE_BYTES)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(b_pack, B_PACK_RANGE_BYTES)
+
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    a_smem = S.make_shared((NUM_WARPS, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((NUM_WARPS, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16)
+
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(A_PACK_K):
+        a_elem_offset = (((tile_row // WARP_M) * A_PACK_K + k_tile) * WARP_SIZE + lane) * 8
+        b_elem_offset = ((k_tile * B_PACK_N + (tile_col // WARP_N)) * WARP_SIZE + lane) * 8
+        a_byte_offset = S.convert(a_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+        b_byte_offset = S.convert(b_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+
+        a_frag_g = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, a_byte_offset, 0)
+        b_frag_g = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_byte_offset, 0)
+
+        a_frag_view = S.view(a_frag_g, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag_view = S.view(b_frag_g, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))

+        for frag_half in S.range(2):

+                a_smem[warp, lane, frag_half * 4 + frag_elem] = a_frag_view[frag_half, frag_elem, 0]
+                b_smem[warp, lane, frag_half * 4 + frag_elem] = b_frag_view[frag_half, frag_elem, 0]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag_view[0], b_frag_view[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag_view[1], b_frag_view[1], acc)

+        S.syncthreads()

 HARDTANH_MAX = 2.0
 EPS = 1e-05
 
+WARP_SIZE = 64
+NUM_WARPS = 4
+BLOCK_THREADS = WARP_SIZE * NUM_WARPS
+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+WARP_M = 32
+WARP_N = 32
+K_TILE = 16
+
+A_PACK_M = BATCH_SIZE // WARP_M
+A_PACK_K = IN_FEATURES // K_TILE
+B_PACK_K = IN_FEATURES // K_TILE
+B_PACK_N = OUT_FEATURES // WARP_N
+
+A_PACK_RANGE_BYTES = A_PACK_M * A_PACK_K * WARP_SIZE * 8 * 2
+B_PACK_RANGE_BYTES = B_PACK_K * B_PACK_N * WARP_SIZE * 8 * 2
+
+
+def _launch_gemm():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (BLOCK_THREADS, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _launch_post():
+    return ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))

+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_mfma_kernel(
+    a_pack: S.Tensor((A_PACK_M, A_PACK_K, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16),
+    b_pack: S.Tensor((B_PACK_K, B_PACK_N, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16),
+    bias: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WARP_SIZE
+    warp = tid // WARP_SIZE
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2
+
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    tile_row = block_row + warp_row * WARP_M
+    tile_col = block_col + warp_col * WARP_N
+
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(a_pack, A_PACK_RANGE_BYTES)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(b_pack, B_PACK_RANGE_BYTES)
+
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    a_smem = S.make_shared((NUM_WARPS, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16)
+    b_smem = S.make_shared((NUM_WARPS, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16)
+
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(A_PACK_K):
+        a_elem_offset = (((tile_row // WARP_M) * A_PACK_K + k_tile) * WARP_SIZE + lane) * 8
+        b_elem_offset = ((k_tile * B_PACK_N + (tile_col // WARP_N)) * WARP_SIZE + lane) * 8
+        a_byte_offset = S.convert(a_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+        b_byte_offset = S.convert(b_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+
+        a_frag_g = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, a_byte_offset, 0)
+        b_frag_g = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_byte_offset, 0)
+
+        a_frag_view = S.view(a_frag_g, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag_view = S.view(b_frag_g, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        for frag_half in S.range(2):
+            for frag_elem in S.range(4):
+                a_smem[warp, lane, frag_half * 4 + frag_elem] = a_frag_view[frag_half, frag_elem, 0]
+                b_smem[warp, lane, frag_half * 4 + frag_elem] = b_frag_view[frag_half, frag_elem, 0]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag_view[0], b_frag_view[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag_view[1], b_frag_view[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    lane_col = lane % 32
+    lane_row_quad = lane // 32
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        out_col = tile_col + lane_col
+        out_row = tile_row + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * lane_row_quad + (acc_idx % 4)
+        value = acc[acc_idx] + S.convert(bias[out_col], S.f32)
+        y[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(value, S.bf16)

The current A packing may be over-separating the two MFMA halves. I’m trying the simpler contiguous-8 chunk layout for A while keeping the current B layout, because that aligns better with the “natural order from one 16-byte fragment” requirement.
